2:19:446:19:12:82:515:634:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:A:The  use  of  chain-linked  methods  reduces  significantly  the  problem  of  price  structure  obsolescence 
2:20:556:12:13:82:515:622:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:A:present in fixed base environments. However, price updating introduces a new dimension that may 
2:21:652:13:12:82:515:609:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:A:produce  confusion  if  not  accounted  for.  Probably  the  most  notorious  difficulty  generated  by  the 
2:22:761:12:12:82:515:597:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:A:introduction of chain-linked indices to the measurement of GDP has been that the aggregate is not 
2:23:859:12:13:82:514:585:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:A:the  direct  sum  of  its  components,  thus not  only making  it  harder  to  explain  its  behaviour but  also 
2:24:971:13:12:82:511:572:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:A:making  it  more  cumbersome  to  work  with  the  series  in  a  consistent  manner.  Because  of  the  non-
2:25:1080:12:12:82:515:560:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:A:additivity  of  the  components,  one  of  the  processes  that  have  been  affected  is  that  of  the  indirect 
2:26:1195:12:13:82:514:548:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:A:seasonal adjustment. This document presents a consistent framework to identify and track down the 
2:27:1291:13:12:82:514:535:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:A:sources of seasonal effects to its components in an aggregate measure chain-linked using the annual 
2:28:1386:12:13:82:515:523:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:A:overlap method.  This  is  done based  on  the  decomposition  of  component’s  contributions  and  the 
2:29:1489:13:12:82:511:510:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:A:indirect seasonal adjustment. The framework allows separating the effects on growth rates into non-
2:30:1588:12:400:82:457:498:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:A:systematic seasonal effects, systematic seasonality and changes in systematic seasonality.

3:34:1973:0:18:71:166:759:122:g_d0_f9:122:g_d0_f9:C:1. Introduction 
3:35:1987:18:12:53:544:741:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:Macroeconomic  analysis  devotes  a  fair  amount  of  effort  to  the  economy’s real  variables, thus generating a  need 
3:36:2106:12:13:53:543:729:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:for  aggregate  measurements of  volumes  and  quantities.  When  evaluating  the  economy’s  performance, Gross 
3:37:2217:13:12:53:543:716:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:Domestic Product (GDP) is the most often used indicator. Traditionally, GDP and other real variables have been 
3:38:2328:12:12:53:543:704:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:measured using the fixed-base-year method; however, in the last  decades its shortcomings have become obvious 
3:39:2438:12:13:53:242:692:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:and difficult to ignore (Steindel, 1995).         
3:40:2486:13:12:53:56:679:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B: 
3:41:2486:12:13:53:543:667:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:In line with the recommendations of the System of National Accounts (SNA, 1993) many countries have moved 
3:42:2591:13:12:53:540:654:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:to  an  annual  update  of  the  relative  price  structure  for their real  output  series through  the  generation  of  chain-
3:43:2717:12:12:53:543:642:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:linked  series.  This  procedure  greatly  reduces  the  problem  of  price  structure  obsolescence but  introduces  a  new 
3:44:2841:12:13:53:544:630:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:dimension into the analysis that makes understanding the evolution of the series less straightforward. Probably the 
3:45:2953:13:12:53:540:617:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:most  notorious  difficulty  has  been  that  an  aggregate  is  not  the  direct  sum  of  its  components,  known  as  non-
3:46:3078:12:12:53:544:605:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:additivity, and therefore the fixed base accounting identities do not hold for the chain-linked levels. This induces 
3:47:3195:12:13:53:544:593:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:some  practical issues, makes  working  with  the  series  less  straightforward and may blur  the  analysis. It  is 
3:48:3307:13:12:53:544:580:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:unadvisable, however, to ignore  the  fact  and continue  working  as  if  the  accounting  properties  of  the  fixed  base 
3:49:3432:12:13:53:544:568:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:methodology  are  still  valid because it could  lead  to significant error if  the environment  has  suffered relevant 
3:50:3548:13:12:53:254:555:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:changes in its price structure (OECD, 2006a).  
3:51:3594:12:12:53:56:543:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B: 
3:52:3594:12:13:53:544:531:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:In  this  context  all  processes  that  rely  on  the  fixed-base  accounting  identities,  like  the  case  of  the  national 
3:53:3722:13:12:53:543:518:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:accounting identities  of  GDP, may  be  affected  to  a  varying  degree.  Cobb  (2014a)  illustrates  this in  a  forecasting 
3:54:3850:12:12:53:543:506:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:context showing that the discrepancy between an aggregate forecast generated by proper chain-linking and the one 
3:55:3959:12:13:53:543:494:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:resulting of using the fixed-base identities directly may be significant and that these differences due to inaccurate 
3:56:4075:13:12:53:544:481:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:aggregation are not necessarily small compared to the forecasting error. Another process that could be affected is 
3:57:4190:12:13:53:182:469:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:indirect seasonal adjustment.  
3:58:4220:13:12:53:56:456:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B: 
3:59:4220:12:12:53:543:444:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:The  process  of  seasonal  adjustment  is  performed  to  aid  economic  analysis  in  uncovering  the  underlying 
3:60:4336:12:13:53:544:432:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:movements of a series by removing systematic intra-annual movements and other effects  that contribute to hide 
3:61:4447:13:12:53:544:419:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:them. There  are  a  number  of  approaches  and  methods  used  to  perform  this  task.  One  of  them,  the indirect 
3:62:4566:12:12:53:543:407:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:seasonal adjustment, involves generating the aggregate from the seasonal adjustment of its components. By doing 
3:63:4676:12:13:53:544:395:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:so, this  method generates  an aggregate that is  consistent  with  the  adjusted  components  and,  therefore,  the 
3:64:4789:13:12:53:543:382:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:aggregate  performance may  be  broken  down precisely to  be  accounted for  by  the  components. This  means  that 
3:65:4904:12:13:53:544:370:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:specific developments  may  be tracked  down  to  their  source  and given  a  meaningful  explanation. The  loss  of 
3:66:5019:13:12:53:535:357:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:additivity due to the adoption of the chain-linked method, however, makes this process more cumbersome.1        
3:67:5127:12:12:53:56:345:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B: 
3:68:5127:12:13:53:544:333:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:To alleviate the  problem  of  explaining a  chain-linked aggregate’s performance  in  terms  of its components, 
3:69:5236:13:12:53:543:320:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:publishing bodies generally  accompany  the  aggregate  measure  with the  contributions  of  each  component to  its 
3:70:5351:12:12:53:544:308:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:growth, where these contributions do sum up to the total. These contributions have become the standard way of 
3:71:5460:12:13:53:543:296:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:breaking down the performance of an aggregate and in this document we rely on them to break down the seasonal 
3:72:5570:13:12:53:544:283:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:effects of  an  aggregate  measure so  they  can  be  explained  based  on  the  properties  of  the  individual  components. 
3:73:5696:12:13:53:544:271:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:Section 2 briefly explains the process of seasonal adjustment and the identification the seasonal effects for a series 
3:74:5811:13:12:53:543:258:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:that is adjusted directly. Section 3 presents a framework for obtaining consistent indirectly adjusted aggregates in 
3:75:5926:12:12:53:544:246:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:the context of the annual overlap methodology. Section 4 presents the derivation necessary to identify the sources 
3:76:6041:12:13:53:544:234:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:of seasonal effects in a annual overlap chain-linked aggregate. Section 5 presents an example for the identification 
3:77:6155:13:13:53:434:221:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:of seasonal effects using Chilean GDP data and Section 6 summarizes the main findings. 
3:78:6241:13:12:53:56:208:122:g_d0_f11:122:g_d0_f11:C: 
3:79:6241:12:13:53:56:196:122:g_d0_f11:122:g_d0_f11:C: 
3:80:6241:13:18:72:514:183:122:g_d0_f9:122:g_d0_f9:C:2. Direct seasonal adjustment and identifying the seasonal effects involved  
3:81:6315:18:13:53:544:165:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:Time  series  are  at  the  heart  of  economic  analysis  and  policy  decision.  However,  often  relevant  series  exhibit 
3:82:6441:13:12:53:544:152:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:systematic patterns and other effects that mask their underlying movement. When these movements are the focus 
3:83:6550:12:12:53:543:140:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:of  interest,  it  is  common  to  try  to  identify and remove  these  patterns  and  effects  in  order  to allow  for  a  more 
3:84:6677:12:13:53:159:128:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:straightforward analysis. 
3:85:6702:13:18:53:59:115:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:  
3:86:6702:18:9:53:200:97:122:g_d0_f6:122:g_d0_f6:C:                                                           
3:87:6760:9:14:53:540:88:42:g_d0_f8:99:g_d0_f8:F:1 It is worth noting that other approaches to seasonal adjustment methods may be preferred when disaggregate consistency is 
3:88:6883:14:0:54:105:74:99:g_d0_f8:99:g_d0_f6:F:not required. 
4:89:6897:0:18:89:279:760:122:g_d0_f7:122:g_d0_f7:C:2.1. Seasonal adjustment of a time-series 
4:90:6937:18:13:53:544:742:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:The seasonal adjustment process relies on the assumption that a time-series may be expressed as a combination of 
4:91:7050:13:12:53:543:729:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:three  distinctive  unobservable  components,  where  one  of  them  reflects  all  the  seasonal  movements.  The  other 
4:92:7172:12:13:53:544:717:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:two components are the trend and the irregular component, where the first reflects the underlying movement of 
4:93:7282:13:12:53:544:704:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:the series and its general direction while the second contains all the erratic behaviour, both the regular unexplained 
4:94:7401:12:12:53:543:692:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:non-systematic  movement  and  specific,  normally  significant,  non-periodic  shocks  that  may  result  from  natural 
4:95:7522:12:13:53:160:680:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:disasters or civil events.  
4:96:7548:13:12:53:56:667:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B: 
4:97:7548:12:12:53:544:655:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:The seasonal component  reflects  the movement  that is attributable to the features of  a given period  and may be 
4:98:7663:12:13:53:544:643:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:separated  into  systematic  and non-systematic.  The  systematic  portion contains  the  intra-annual  fluctuations  that 
4:99:7786:13:12:53:544:630:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:occur regularly every year. They are generally associated with weather conditions or certain aspects of the specific 
4:100:7900:12:13:53:544:618:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:season. An example is an increase in the consumption of heating oil in winter. The non-systematic portion refers 
4:101:8011:13:12:53:544:605:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:to  the  effects  of  differing  daily  composition  of  the  periods  being  compared,  like  number  of  holydays,  working 
4:102:8137:12:12:53:543:593:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:days,  etc. This  component  also  contains  events  that  occur  systematically  but  with  a  frequency  different  form  a 
4:103:8262:12:13:53:543:581:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:year, like leap years that occur every four. An example of the effects or daily composition could be an increase of 
4:104:8375:13:12:53:420:568:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:attendance to theatres and cinemas in months with more weekends and holidays.        
4:105:8458:12:13:53:56:556:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B: 
4:106:8458:13:13:53:543:543:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:Although the components  could interact  in a number  of ways, the standard methods assume that yt, either  in its 
4:107:8573:13:20:53:300:530:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:original form or as a transformation,2 may be written as:   
4:108:8631:20:24:103:545:510:142:g_d0_f13:122:g_d0_f6:C:   ttttty   T  S   K   I (2.1) 
4:109:8664:24:13:53:523:486:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:where Tt  is the trend, St is the systematic seasonality, Kt is the non-systematic seasonality and It is the irregular 
4:110:8776:13:22:53:272:473:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f6:B:component. The seasonally adjusted series is then:  
4:111:8827:22:21:157:545:451:143:g_d0_f15:122:g_d0_f6:C:()         SAttttttyy   S   KT  I (2.2) 
4:112:8870:21:13:53:543:430:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:The outcome of the seasonal adjustment of an example series is presented in Chart 2.1. As it can be appreciated, 
4:113:8981:13:12:53:544:417:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:the trend retains the unadjusted overall growth and level and the seasonal and irregular components are expressed 
4:114:9092:12:8:53:507:405:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:as deviations from it. The seasonally adjusted series is generated as the sum of the trend and the irregular.

4:148:9390:11:13:53:543:167:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:Regarding  the  actual  method  used  to  identify  the  unobserved  components,  there  are  a  number  of  approaches; 
4:149:9511:13:12:53:540:154:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:however,  two  relatively  similar  time  series  methods  stand  out  as  the  most  used.3 One of  them  is  the  non-
4:150:9629:12:13:53:543:142:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:parametric  X12-ARIMA  method (Findley,  et.  al.,  1998) that  relies  on  moving  averages  of  different  lengths  to 
4:151:9749:13:21:53:543:129:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:identify the components and the other is the parametric TRAMO-SEATS (Gómez and Maravall, 1997) that tries 
4:152:9853:21:9:53:200:108:122:g_d0_f6:122:g_d0_f6:C:                                                           
4:153:9911:9:11:53:300:99:42:g_d0_f8:99:g_d0_f6:F:2 Economic series in levels are typically modelled in logarithms. 
4:154:9975:11:14:53:529:88:42:g_d0_f8:99:g_d0_f8:F:3 Foldesi et al. (2007) provide a complete survey of the different methods. OECD (2009) presents a survey of the methods 
4:155:10095:14:0:54:234:74:99:g_d0_f8:99:g_d0_f8:F:that are used in each of the OECD countries.  
5:156:10141:0:12:53:543:760:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:to  identify  a  unique  model  for  each  component. Although, both  methods  are  based  on  different  theoretical 
5:157:10258:12:13:53:543:748:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:assumptions,  in  practice  they  are  very  similar.  In  fact,  in  the  more  recent  implementations  both  methods  have 
5:158:10384:13:12:53:543:735:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:relied  on  the  same  procedure  to  identify  models  and  perform  prior  adjustments  and  only  differ  in  the  actual 
5:159:10509:12:13:53:540:723:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:unobserved  component  identification.  In  the  most  recent  release of  the  X12-ARIMA  family, that  is  the X13-
5:160:10624:13:12:53:543:710:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:ARIMA-SEATS (U.S.  Census  Bureau,  2013); both  methods  are  contained  in  the  same  program  and  may  be 
5:161:10733:12:12:53:544:698:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:chosen  depending  on  the  analyst’s  preference. For  the  purpose  of  this  document  both  methods  provide  the 
5:162:10850:12:13:53:167:686:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:necessary information.4     
5:163:10877:13:12:53:56:673:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B: 
5:164:10877:12:18:89:311:661:122:g_d0_f7:122:g_d0_f7:C:2.2. Identifying seasonal effects in a time-series 
5:165:10926:18:13:53:544:643:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:In the process of analysing time-series one would typically wish to be able to identify the different effects that are 
5:166:11045:13:12:53:543:630:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:at play. When examining a series, one might wonder how much of the level in a certain period is solely due to a 
5:167:11157:12:13:53:543:618:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:seasonal  phenomenon  and what  is  responsible  for  it.  When  analysing  the  economy’s  performance,  on  the  other 
5:168:11278:13:12:53:544:605:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:hand, one might be more interested in knowing how much of the registered growth is only due to seasonal factors 
5:169:11390:12:12:53:543:593:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:or  how  much  is  due  to  the  specific  calendar  composition  of  the  examined  period.  At  least  in  regards  to  these 
5:170:11518:12:13:53:393:581:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:factors, the seasonal adjustment process allows to separate a number of effects. 
5:171:11597:13:12:53:59:568:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:  
5:172:11597:12:12:53:544:556:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f14:B:Recalling expression (2.1), we have that a series may be written as the sum of its trend, its systematic seasonality, 
5:173:11714:12:14:53:544:544:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:its non-systematic seasonality and its irregular component, and that the seasonally adjusted series is simply the sum 
5:174:11830:14:13:53:544:530:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:of  the  trend  and  the  irregular  component.  By  comparing  the  behaviour  of  both  series,  that  is yt and ytSA,  it  is 
5:175:11958:13:12:53:544:517:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:possible to determine how important the seasonal effects are. Regarding the level of a series at any point in time t, 
5:176:12075:12:13:53:544:505:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:it is only necessary to look at the ratio between the both to obtain the percentage of the original that is estimated 
5:177:12193:13:12:53:543:492:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:to  be  seasonal  and  by  comparing  the  growth  rates  of  both  series  over  an  interval  it  is  possible  to  obtain  the 
5:178:12323:12:28:53:377:480:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:percentage points of growth that are attributable to seasonal factors, that is: 
5:179:12402:28:11:156:145:452:118:g_d0_f15:40:g_d0_f12:F:1SAttSA
5:180:12409:11:0:137:139:441:40:g_d0_f12:40:g_d0_f12:F:t
5:181:12410:0:7:135:140:459:118:g_d0_f12:118:g_d0_f12:F:y

6:240:14294:12:13:53:544:710:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:becomes apparent when looking at annual change, because one would expect yearly growth rates to be unaffected 
6:241:14404:13:12:53:504:697:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:by the systematic seasonal effects. If the systematic seasonality evolves, however, it is not entirely neutral. 
6:242:14515:12:12:53:56:685:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:

6:244:14637:13:12:53:544:660:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:components of  expression  (2.1) are unobservable  and  need to  be  estimated  from  the  data.  This  means  that they 
6:245:14755:12:13:53:544:648:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:may change with the addition of new information. For the purpose of this document we will confine the change

6:247:14989:13:13:53:544:622:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:difference between the deviation estimated for t-s in t-s and the one estimated for t-s using the data available up

7:333:18954:12:18:72:518:602:122:g_d0_f9:122:g_d0_f9:C:3. Indirect seasonal adjustment of an annual overlap chain-linked aggregate  
7:334:19029:18:13:53:543:584:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:The  process  of  seasonal  adjustment  is  performed  to  aid  economic  analysis  in  uncovering  the  underlying 
7:335:19145:13:12:53:544:571:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:movements of a series by removing systematic intra-annual movements and other effects  that contribute to hide 
7:336:19256:12:13:53:544:559:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:them. The  approaches  and  methods  used will  depend  on  which  is  the  most  appropriate  for the final objective. 
7:337:19374:13:12:53:543:546:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:When it comes to explaining economic performance, the indirect seasonal adjustment, which involves generating 
7:338:19484:12:12:53:544:534:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:the adjusted aggregate from the seasonal adjustment of its  components, generates an aggregate that is  consistent 
7:339:19596:12:13:53:544:522:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:with its components.  This  means  the  aggregate  performance  may  be  broken  down  to  be  accounted  for  by  the 
7:340:19715:13:12:53:544:509:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:components and, therefore, that developments may be given a meaningful explanation. The loss of additivity due 
7:341:19824:12:12:53:544:497:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:to  the  adoption  of  the  chain-linked  method,  however,  makes  this  process  more  cumbersome. By  following  a 
7:342:19941:12:13:53:544:485:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:procedure analogous to that of the non-adjusted series, it is possible to generate a chain-linked seasonally adjusted 
7:343:20058:13:12:53:102:472:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:aggregate.6 
7:344:20069:12:13:53:56:460:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B: 
7:345:20069:13:18:89:328:447:122:g_d0_f7:122:g_d0_f7:C:3.1. The annual overlap method for quarterly series 
7:346:20118:18:12:53:544:429:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:There  are  various  methodologies  to  implement  the  annual  update of  prices being  the  annual  overlap  method  of 
7:347:20240:12:13:53:544:417:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:Laspeyres indices one of the more popular ones. This technique involves creating a set of fixed-base overlapping 
7:348:20352:13:14:53:544:404:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:links  with a  length  of  two years,  where  in each link  both  the  quantities  of  the relevant  year  (y)  and  the previous 
7:349:20482:14:12:53:543:390:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:one (y-1) are valued using average prices of the previous year (y-1). Then, using the growth rates of these links an 
7:350:20599:12:12:53:544:378:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:annual time  series  is  built  starting  from  the  first  link. The  quarterly  series are  then built  based  on  the  annual 
7:351:20726:12:26:53:530:366:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:structures in a consistent way.7 That means that the quarterly aggregate may be expressed in the following way:

7:391:21727:12:14:53:544:166:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:components. This means that to build a chain-linked aggregate it is only necessary to have the quarterly real series

7:393:21895:21:9:53:200:131:122:g_d0_f6:122:g_d0_f6:C:                                                           
7:394:21953:9:12:53:536:122:42:g_d0_f8:99:g_d0_f6:F:6 It is worth noting that direct seasonal adjustment methods may be preferred when disaggregate consistency is not required.

7:397:22231:14:11:54:543:85:99:g_d0_f8:99:g_d0_f8:F:or  as  chain-linked  sub-indices.  These  will  be  referred  to  simply  as  components,  as  opposed  to  variables  valued  at  current 
7:398:22371:11:0:54:357:74:99:g_d0_f8:81:g_d0_f8:F:prices, referred to as nominal, and those valued at previous year annual prices. 
8:399:22452:0:18:89:510:760:122:g_d0_f7:122:g_d0_f7:C:3.2. An indirect method for seasonally adjusting an annual overlap chain-linked aggregate  
8:400:22540:18:13:53:544:742:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:There  are  two  alternatives  to  seasonally  adjust  an  aggregate;  to  obtain  it  by  adjusting  it  directly  or  to  generate  it 
8:401:22677:13:12:53:544:729:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:from  its  seasonally  adjusted  components,  the  indirect  approach.  The discussion on  which  method  is  better  is 
8:402:22797:12:13:53:544:717:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:ongoing and depends crucially on the final objective.9 Anyhow, the indirect method has a very desirable property 
8:403:22909:13:12:53:544:704:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:in  that  it  guarantees  consistency  between the  aggregate and  the components and allows,  therefore,  explaining its 
8:404:23030:12:12:53:217:692:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:performance in terms of the latter.      
8:405:23069:12:13:53:56:680:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B: 
8:406:23069:13:12:53:544:667:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:The  process of  generating the seasonally adjusted aggregate is  very similar to the chain-linking of the unadjusted 
8:407:23187:12:12:53:544:655:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:one. However,  it  is  necessary  to  provide  seasonally  adjusted  nominal  annual  figures that are  consistent  with  the 
8:408:23311:12:13:53:543:643:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:adjusted component  series.  These  adjusted  annual  figures may  differ  slightly  from  the unadjusted.  This may 
8:409:23427:13:12:53:544:630:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:initially  seem  counterintuitive due  to  the  fact  that one  would  expect the systematic  portion  of  the  seasonal 
8:410:23546:12:13:53:543:618:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:component to cancel out within a year, however, the non-systematic portion does not necessarily. Fortunately, the 
8:411:23658:13:12:53:544:605:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:process of adjusting the components provides the necessary information to be able to  construct these seasonally 
8:412:23769:12:12:53:544:593:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:adjusted  nominal  annual  series. It  is  only  necessary  to  make  the  reasonable  assumption  that  the annual implicit 
8:413:23891:12:13:53:543:581:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:price deflators are not affected by the non-systematic seasonal component. Based on this assumption and that the 
8:414:24004:13:12:53:544:568:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:seasonal  adjustment  program  provides  the  systematic  and  non-systematic  seasonal  component  separately,  it  is 
8:415:24124:12:11:53:513:556:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:fairly straightforward to aggregate the seasonally adjusted components. Chart 3.1 shows the process.            
8:416:24234:11:12:54:56:545:99:g_d0_f7:99:g_d0_f7:F:

8:423:24351:11:13:72:356:275:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f6:A:1- The unadjusted quarterly components are seasonally adjusted.  
8:424:24414:13:12:72:544:262:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:A:2- The  component’s  unadjusted  annual  price  deflators  are  obtained  by  dividing  the  unadjusted  annual 
8:425:24525:12:13:89:349:250:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f6:A:nominal components by the annual unadjusted components. 
8:426:24580:13:12:72:544:237:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:A:3- The adjusted annual nominal components are obtained by multiplying the annual adjusted components by 
8:427:24683:12:12:89:296:225:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f6:A:the respective unadjusted annual price deflators. 
8:428:24732:12:13:72:544:213:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:A:4- The   adjusted   annual   nominal   aggregate   is   obtained   by   adding   up   the   adjusted   annual   nominal 
8:429:24851:13:12:89:147:200:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f6:A:components. 
8:430:24862:12:12:72:544:188:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:A:5- The  adjusted quarterly components are valued at previous year prices using the component’s  unadjusted 
8:431:24968:12:13:89:186:176:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f6:A:annual price deflators. 
8:432:24991:13:12:72:544:163:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:A:6- The  adjusted  quarterly  aggregate  valued  at  previous  year  prices  is  generated  by  adding  the  adjusted 
8:433:25107:12:13:89:315:151:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f6:A:quarterly components valued at previous year prices. 
8:434:25159:13:12:72:544:138:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:A:7- The  adjusted  quarterly  chain-linked  aggregate  is  obtained  by  dividing  the  adjusted  quarterly  aggregate 
8:435:25276:12:12:89:544:126:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:A:valued at previous year prices by the previous year adjusted annual aggregate price deflator. This deflator 
8:436:25384:12:13:89:544:114:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:A:is  obtained  from  dividing  the  adjusted  annual  nominal  aggregate  by  the  adjusted  annual  chain-linked 
8:437:25497:13:15:89:134:101:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f6:A:aggregate. 
8:438:25507:15:9:53:200:86:122:g_d0_f6:122:g_d0_f6:C:                                                           
8:439:25565:9:0:53:282:77:42:g_d0_f8:99:g_d0_f8:F:9 Astolfi (2001) provides a brief exposition on the subject.  
9:440:25625:0:12:53:544:760:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:This  procedure  allows  to  generate  the  aggregate  seasonally  adjusted  series  but  it  may  also  be  used  to  build  the 
9:441:25755:12:13:53:543:748:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:intermediate aggregate series that are needed to identify the seasonal effects, which are the original series excluding 
9:442:25875:13:13:53:444:735:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:non-systematic seasonality and the series adjusted using the previous year seasonal pattern.  
9:443:25968:13:13:53:55:722:122:g_d0_f6:122:g_d0_f6:C: 
9:444:25968:13:13:53:56:709:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B: 
9:445:25968:13:13:72:545:696:122:g_d0_f9:122:g_d0_f9:C:4. Explaining  aggregate  unobserved  components  in  terms  of  the  dissagregate 
9:446:26050:13:18:89:127:683:122:g_d0_f9:122:g_d0_f9:C:series 
9:447:26056:18:12:53:543:665:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:When it  comes  to  analysing  an  aggregate  time  series,  the  same  questions  regarding  seasonal  influences  on  the 
9:448:26180:12:13:53:544:653:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:different measures may arise. However, the composite nature of the aggregate means  that the aggregate seasonal 
9:449:26291:13:12:53:544:640:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:effects are  not  the result of  the  economy’s  response to  changing circumstances but are a  combination  of  effects 
9:450:26411:12:12:53:544:628:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:sourced  in  the  underlying  component’s  movements and,  therefore,  an  explanation  for  aggregate  performance 
9:451:26526:12:13:53:544:616:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:should ideally be rooted in the specifics of the components. This makes being able to track down the sources of 
9:452:26638:13:12:53:186:603:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:the aggregate effects desirable. 
9:453:26670:12:12:53:56:591:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B: 
9:454:26670:12:13:53:543:579:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:As with any chain-linked aggregate, however, the seasonally adjusted aggregate will not be equal to the sum of the 
9:455:26784:13:12:53:543:566:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:seasonally adjusted components making the breakdown less straightforward. This difficulty is fairly easy to tackle 
9:456:26896:12:13:53:544:554:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:when  analysing  the  levels  and  for  growth  rates, as  with  the  unadjusted  series, the contributions may  be  used  to 
9:457:27020:13:12:53:329:541:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:explain the aggregate performance in terms of the components.  
9:458:27081:12:12:53:56:529:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:

9:460:27148:19:12:53:543:498:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:The analysis of the aggregate level is not very different from that of a component’s only that, to be able to break it 
9:461:27267:12:12:53:544:486:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:down  to  the  component  level, the  annual  updating  of  relative  prices  must  be  accounted  for.  Starting  from

9:515:28413:28:13:53:543:208:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:As it can be seen, both expressions simply reflect the difference between the component’s levels in each measure

9:521:28923:18:13:53:543:127:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:With  the  adoption  of  chain-linking, explaining  aggregate  growth  in  terms  of  the  components  has  become  less 
9:522:29043:13:12:53:544:114:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:straightforward  due  to  the  annual  change  in  the  structure  of  relative  prices.  In  this  context,  contributions  have 
9:523:29173:12:13:53:544:102:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:become  the  standard  way  of  breaking  down  the  performance  of  a chain-linked aggregate;  however,  the  way  of 
9:524:29291:13:12:53:543:89:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:calculating  these  contributions is  not  unique  and  depends  on  which  of  the annual  chain-linking  methods  is 
9:525:29409:12:0:53:544:77:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:implemented. In  the  case  of  contributions  to  quarterly  growth,  IMF  (2001)  provides  a  unique  formula  for  the 
10:526:29533:0:12:53:544:760:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:quarterly overlap  technique  but  none  for  the annual overlap  technique. This  is  probably  due  to  the  fact  that 
10:527:29655:12:13:53:499:748:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:finding the right weights that permit the quarterly contributions to sum up to the total is far from direct. 
10:528:29761:13:12:53:56:735:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B: 
10:529:29761:12:13:53:543:723:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:This is quite inconvenient given  that the annual overlap method is the most popular  method in the OECD.10 In 
10:530:29871:13:12:53:544:710:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:this context, according to Eurostat (2008), at least six different formulas have been proposed to fill this gap. Some 
10:531:29988:12:12:53:543:698:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:countries find the contributions from using pair of years valued at the first year’s prices. Others,  like France and 
10:532:30104:12:13:53:544:686:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:Germany  have  proposed  their  own  way. The OECD simply  relies  on an  approximation  to  calculate its  global 
10:533:30215:13:12:53:544:673:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:contributions  acknowledging  that  it  is  not right  in  a  strict  sense  (OECD,  2013). The measures presented  in 
10:534:30330:12:12:53:544:661:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:Eurostat  (2008) are basically a compromise between  user  friendliness,  interpretability  and  core  properties.  The 
10:535:30448:12:13:53:543:649:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:problem  with all  but  one  of them is  that they  do  not  necessarily produce  additive  contributions.  This  core 
10:536:30567:13:12:53:544:636:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:property is fundamental when contributions are to be calculated as a difference and this, as it will become obvious 
10:537:30683:12:13:53:331:624:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:later on, is a necessary feature for the identifications of effects.    
10:538:30754:13:12:53:56:611:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:

10:540:30872:12:13:53:544:587:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:French Quarterly  National  Accounts (INSEE,  2007).11 More  recently the  Chilean  Quarterly  National  Accounts 
10:541:30984:13:12:53:544:574:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:have  adopted  a  similar  measure  suggested in Cobb  (2013),  which  is  also  additive. Either  measure  fulfil  the 
10:542:31103:12:12:53:543:562:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:necessary  requirements  to  be  used  for  the  analysis  of  the  following  sections,  however,  the  measure  proposed  in 
10:543:31230:12:13:53:543:550:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:INSEE  (2007)  does  show  some  undesirable  properties  under  seasonality  or  strong  volatility  and,  therefore,  we 
10:544:31353:13:12:53:306:537:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:proceed by using the measure suggested in Cobb (2013).12

10:611:32869:9:14:53:529:189:42:g_d0_f8:99:g_d0_f8:F:10 According to the last available survey of OECD (2009) updated to May 2014, out of the 37 OECD countries plus Brazil 
10:612:32987:14:11:54:537:175:99:g_d0_f8:99:g_d0_f8:F:and Russian Federation, 27 use the annual overlap method, 5 use the quarterly overlap method, 4 use an unspecified indirect 
10:613:33111:11:11:54:527:164:99:g_d0_f8:99:g_d0_f8:F:method and one still uses a fixed-base method. It’s worth mentioning that the five countries that use the quarterly overlap 
10:614:33234:11:11:54:520:153:99:g_d0_f8:99:g_d0_f8:F:method are Australia, Canada, Japan, United Kingdom and United States. The popularity is probably due to its desirable 
10:615:33353:11:12:54:519:142:99:g_d0_f8:99:g_d0_f8:F:temporal aggregation properties. Annual figures are the simple sum of the quarterly figures. With the Quarterly Overlap 
10:616:33471:12:8:54:339:130:99:g_d0_f8:99:g_d0_f6:F:method, if consistency is required, a benchmarking procedure is required. 
10:617:33543:8:12:53:362:122:42:g_d0_f8:99:g_d0_f6:F:11 The same measure is used by Belgium (Banque Nationale de Belgique, 2010).

11:696:36101:13:12:53:544:210:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:chain-linking  for  its  accounts  in  2012  and  implemented  the  annual  overlap  method  for  Laspeyres  indices

11:698:36345:13:12:53:380:185:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:2013). For the purpose of this exercise we used quarterly production data.14  
11:699:36420:12:12:53:56:173:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:

11:702:36656:27:8:53:200:121:122:g_d0_f6:122:g_d0_f6:C:                                                           
11:703:36714:8:16:53:513:113:42:g_d0_f6:99:g_d0_f8:F:14 The level of aggregation is the following; Agriculture, forestry and fishery, Mining, Manufacturing and the Rest. The 
11:704:36833:16:12:54:534:97:99:g_d0_f8:99:g_d0_f8:F:selection of components is done specifically to allow for a diversity of seasonal patterns and effects among components but 
11:705:36957:12:11:54:543:85:99:g_d0_f8:99:g_d0_f8:F:maintaining only a reduced number of them. It is worth mentioning that we perform a default seasonal adjustment in order to 
11:706:37081:11:0:54:468:74:99:g_d0_f8:99:g_d0_f6:F:have the separate unobserved components and, therefore, it will not coincide with the official publication.  
12:707:37191:0:12:53:543:760:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:timings. Agriculture, forestry and fishery, for example, peaks in the first quarter while for the Rest that quarter is a

14:883:46928:0:81:234:515:266:90:g_d0_f16:90:g_d0_f16:F:Annual GrowthContributionsSeasonal Effects
14:884:46970:81:11:541:543:185:122:g_d0_f6:122:g_d0_f6:C: 
14:885:46970:11:12:53:55:174:122:g_d0_f6:122:g_d0_f6:C: 
14:886:46970:12:13:53:543:162:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:The  difference  between  the  original  and  adjusted  growth  rates  is  +0.55  pp.  From  looking  at  the  calculated 
14:887:47092:13:12:53:543:149:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:seasonal  effects, the  first  thing  that  becomes  obvious  is  the  relatively  large  non-systematic  effects  in  Mining, 
14:888:47218:12:12:53:543:137:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:Manufacturing and the Rest that account for more than the total difference (+0.88 pp.). To have solid explanation 
14:889:47332:12:13:53:543:125:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:for this effect would require digging deeper into each sector. It is probable that, to some extent, the effect is due 
14:890:47450:13:12:53:544:112:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:to  2012  being  a  leap year  and  that  Easter  fell  in  April  meaning  three  extra  working  days  relative  to  an  average 
14:891:47580:12:13:53:544:100:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:quarter. The compositional effects work in the opposite direction reducing the gap by -0.32 pp. From examining 
14:892:47691:13:12:53:544:87:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:the  seasonal  level of  the  first  quarter  relative  to  the  yearly average,  we  observe  that  Agriculture  is  at  its  seasonal 
14:893:47827:12:0:53:543:75:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:high while Mining and the Rest are at a seasonal trough. This means that, in principle, Agriculture’s performance 
15:894:47943:0:12:53:544:760:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:affects  the  original  relatively  more  than  the  adjusted  series  while  for  the other  two  sectors  it  is  the  other  way 
15:895:48075:12:13:53:543:748:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:around.17 This  can  be  appreciated  for  Agriculture  that  falls  6%  after  removing  the  non-systematic  effect  and 
15:896:48197:13:12:53:543:735:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:contributes -0.38 pp. to original growth and -0.20 pp. to adjusted aggregate growth. This is observable to a lesser 
15:897:48313:12:13:53:543:723:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:degree for the Rest that grows 6.8% contributing +4.66 pp. to original growth and +4.76 pp. to adjusted growth. 
15:898:48425:13:12:53:543:710:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:Finally, small changes in the component’s seasonal patterns do occur, but nearly cancel each other out making the 
15:899:48539:12:12:53:164:698:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:total effect negligible.       
15:900:48569:12:13:53:56:686:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B: 
15:901:48569:13:12:53:543:673:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:It  is  worth  noting, that  the findings  regarding  the  relative  importance  of  each effect  are  specific  to  this  example 
15:902:48700:12:12:53:436:661:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:and therefore may not be directly generalized to other datasets. The method however is.   
15:903:48789:12:14:53:56:649:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B: 
15:904:48789:14:18:72:173:635:122:g_d0_f9:122:g_d0_f9:C:6. Final remarks 
15:905:48804:18:12:53:544:617:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:The use of chain-linked methods reduces significantly the problem of price structure obsolescence present in fixed 
15:906:48919:12:12:53:544:605:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:base  environments,  but introduces  a  new  dimension  that  may  produce  confusion  if  not  accounted  for. The 
15:907:49035:12:13:53:544:593:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:updating of the economy’s price structure results in lack of additivity for the levels of the series. This means that 
15:908:49153:13:12:53:543:580:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:the  traditional  accounting  identities  are  not  directly  applicable  and,  therefore,  explaining  aggregate  performance 
15:909:49280:12:13:53:269:568:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:from the disaggregate data is not straightforward.  
15:910:49331:13:12:53:56:555:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B: 
15:911:49331:12:12:53:543:543:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:This document presents a consistent framework to identify the sources of seasonal effects in an aggregate measure 
15:912:49443:12:13:53:543:531:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:chain-linked using   the annual overlap method and  adjusted   through   the   indirect  method.  Based   on   the 
15:913:49557:13:12:53:544:518:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:decomposition of component’s contributions, the framework allows separating by industry the contribution of the 
15:914:49669:12:12:53:543:506:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:individual  effects;  that  is  non-systematic  seasonal  effects,  systematic  seasonality  and  the  change  in  systematic 
15:915:49795:12:13:53:107:494:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:seasonality.  
15:916:49808:13:12:53:56:481:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B: 
15:917:49808:12:13:53:544:469:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:It  is  worth  pointing  out  that  the  breakdown  of  the  aggregate  seasonal  effects is  just  a  procedure  based  on  the 
15:918:49937:13:12:53:544:456:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:outcome  of  the seasonal  adjustment  of  the  components.  This  means  that  the  explanation  for  the  aggregates 
15:919:50056:12:12:53:544:444:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:effects will only be meaningful as long as the component’s effects are properly identified and the overall seasonal 
15:920:50171:12:13:53:544:432:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:adjustment  is  acceptable.  In  cases  where  the  adjustment  of  components  is  unreliable  the  use  of  the  indirect 
15:921:50295:13:12:53:543:419:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:seasonal  adjustment  method  may  not  be  advisable and,  therefore,  this  method  of  identifying  the  sources  of 
15:922:50414:12:12:53:543:407:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:aggregate  seasonal  effects  will also  suffer. Being  able  to break  down  the  aggregate  effects,  however,  may  permit 
15:923:50539:12:13:53:544:395:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:tracking down the sources of the effects and validate whether the outcome of the seasonal adjustment process is 
15:924:50649:13:12:53:85:382:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:sound. 
15:925:50655:12:13:53:56:370:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B: 
15:926:50655:13:236:53:57:357:122:g_d0_f9:122:g_d0_f9:C: 
15:927:50655:236:8:53:200:121:122:g_d0_f6:122:g_d0_f6:C:                                                           
15:928:50713:8:16:53:534:113:42:g_d0_f6:99:g_d0_f8:F:17 For chain-linked series the causality is not direct. If the changes in aggregate composition are very small it holds relatively 
15:929:50843:16:12:54:542:97:99:g_d0_f8:99:g_d0_f8:F:well, but chain-linked series are affected by discrete compositional changes due to the updating of relative prices and quarterly 
15:930:50972:12:11:54:527:85:99:g_d0_f8:99:g_d0_f8:F:aggregates built using the annual overlap method also exhibit compositional effects due to the distribution of the updates. 
15:931:51096:11:0:54:404:74:99:g_d0_f8:99:g_d0_f6:F:Annex 4 breaks down the effects even further to account for the chain-linking procedure.

17:975:54901:19:13:53:543:740:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:This technique of annual overlap involves calculating the variation between the current year (y) and the previous 
17:976:55015:13:12:53:543:727:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:year (y-1) both valued using prices of the previous year (y-1) and building a time series from the variation between 
17:977:55132:12:13:53:544:715:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:them.  By  definition,  the  annual  overlap  method  links  a  series  of  consecutive  overlapping  two-period  Laspeyres 
17:978:55256:13:22:53:323:702:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f7:B:indices. Then aggregate growth in any given period is given by:

19:1219:59817:32:13:53:544:444:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:Although the difference between correction terms is quite small, the correction proposed by INSEE (2007) shows 
19:1220:59927:13:12:53:543:431:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:an  undesirable  transfer  of  volatility  under  seasonality  or  strong  volatility. The transfer  occurs  because  the 
19:1221:60048:12:12:53:543:419:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:distribution of the correction term in (A2.1) depends on the relative real importance of the component within the 
19:1222:60161:12:13:53:543:407:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:respective  quarter as  opposed to  the  annual  real  importance.  This means that  the  aggregate correction is 
19:1223:60272:13:12:53:544:394:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:distributed between components according to their relative weights and not based on how much of the aggregate 
19:1224:60380:12:12:53:544:382:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:volatility  comes from  each. The  measure proposed by Cobb  (2013) confines  volatility  to  the contribution of  the 
19:1225:60498:12:13:53:485:370:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:components that presents it. This annex highlights this point through a simple comparative example.

24:1706:73232:13:12:53:56:746:122:g_d0_f15:122:g_d0_f15:C: 
24:1707:73232:12:12:53:543:734:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:In  the  chain-linking  framework the  aggregate  may  be  affected  by  a  number  of  different  effects. In  first  place, in 
24:1708:73361:12:12:53:543:722:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:the  same  way  that  fixed  base  indicators  are  affected,  the  aggregate  may  suffer  compositional  effects  due  to 
24:1709:73485:12:13:53:544:710:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:components growing at different rates. Additionally, the annual update of the structure of relative prices alters its 
24:1710:73603:13:12:53:544:697:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:composition  in  a  discrete  fashion.  These  sudden  changes  may not  only dampen  or  reinforce  the  compositional 
24:1711:73723:12:13:53:543:685:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:effects due to differing component’s growth rates but actually exceed them in magnitude making the overall effect 
24:1712:73837:13:12:53:193:672:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:go in the opposite direction.       
24:1713:73872:12:12:53:56:660:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B: 
24:1714:73872:12:13:53:544:648:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:In  the  context  of  explaining the  seasonal  features  of  chain-linked  series the  problem  arises  from  comparing 
24:1715:73992:13:12:53:544:635:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:periods with different structures of relative prices. Given that many different things may be occurring at the same 
24:1716:74108:12:12:53:546:623:122:g_d0_f8:122:g_d0_f8:B:time, it can be useful to isolate the less intuitive chain-linking effects from the more familiar fixed weight effects.
